42023035	Mbumba ikhakhala penepo , ikhalang'anisa pyonsene pire . Atsogoleri a madjuda akhasingirira Yezu mbalonga tenepa : “ Iye apulumusa anango , mbapulumusikembo ekha ngakhala ndiyedi Kirixtu adasankhulwa na Mulungu . ”
42023036	Anyankhondo akhansingirirambo . Iwo akhafika dhuzi na Yezu mbakhampasa vinyu ya kudjamuka ,
42023037	mbalonga tenepa : “ Ngakhala iwe ndiwe mambo wa madjuda , pulumusika wekha ene ! ”
42023038	Pa ntanda , padzulu pa nsolo wace , pakhadalembwa mafala awa : “ UYU NDI MAMBO WA MADJUDA . ”
42023039	M'bodzi wa mapanga akhadakhomerwa pa ntanda , akhatikanambo Yezu mbalonga tenepa : “ Iwe siwe Kirixtu tayu ? Pulumusika mphapo wekha , mbupulumusambo ife ! ”
42023040	Mbwenye ndzace ansandika mbalonga tenepa : “ Iwe nkhabe gopa Mulungu ? Iwe uli kuthabuswa sawa-sawa ninga iye .
42023041	Ife tina thangwi ya kuthabuswa nayo . Mbwenye iye nkhabe ca kuipa cibodzi cidacita iye . ”
42023042	Na tenepo , alonga kuna Yezu kuti : “ Mbuya , ndikumbukirenimbo mungadza kapita mu Umambo Wanu ! ”
42023043	Yezu atawira tenepa : “ Ndimo mwene ndisakupanga kuti lero , iwe unadza kakhala na ine m'paraizu . ”
42023044	Dhuzi na n'dzidzi utatu wa kumaulo , dziko yonsene yagudumirwa na cidima cikulu , mpaka kufikira n'dzidzi utatu wa ku maulo .
42023045	Dzuwa ya thima , nguwo ikhasitira mbuto ya Mulungu n'Nyumba ya Mulungu , yapanduka pakati-nakati .
42023046	Penepo , Yezu akhuwa na mphambvu , mbalonga tenepa : “ Baba ndiri kupereka nzimu wanga m'manja mwanu . ” Mudamala iye kulonga penepyo , afa .
42023047	Nkulu wa anyakhondo a ku Roma , mudaona iye pidacitika , apasa mbiri Mulungu mbalonga tenepa : “ Ndimo mwene , mamuna uyu akhali wakulungamadi ! ”
42023048	Mbumba yonsene ikhadagumanyikana penepo toera kuona pikhacitika , mudaona iwo penepyo abuluka mbakhamenya cifuwa , na kutsukwala .
42023049	Mbwenye onsene akhandziwa Yezu , na akazi ene akhantowerera kubulukira ku Galileya , akhakhala kutali mbakhalang'anisa pinthu penepi .
42023050	Akhalipo mamuna m'bodzi akhacemerwa Zuze . Iye akhali m'bodzi wa nsoka wa akulu anyakutonga miseru , munthu wadidi na wakulungama .
42023051	Iye akhadakomerwa tayu na kugwandiwa kwa nseru , pontho na pidacita andzace . Zuze akhali wa ku nzinda wa Arimateya , ku Djudeya , iye akhadikhira Umambo wa Mulungu
42023052	Iye aenda kuna Piratu kaphemba manungo a Yezu .
42023053	Na tenepo , aabulusa manungo a Yezu pa ntanda , mbaafinikiza na nguwo yadidi ya kucena . Penepo aaikha nthumbi ibodzi ikhadakumbwa pa mwala , kuti cipo ikhadadzati kuikhwa munthu .
42023054	Penepi pyacitika ntsiku ya cixanu , ntsiku ya kusasanyira , thangwi Sabudu ikhafuna kutoma .
42023055	Akazi akhaperekera Yezu kubulukira ku Galileya , aenda pabodzi na Zuze mbaonambo kuikhwa kudacitwa manungo a Yezu n'nthumbi .
42023056	Buluka penepo , abwerera mbaenda ku nyumba kwawo kasasanyira mafuta akununkhira , toera akhadzodze manungo a Yezu . Mbwenye n'Sabudu , iwo apuma , ninga mukhalongera mwambo .
42024001	Pa ntsiku ya kutoma ya sumana , m'bambakuca , akazi aenda ku nthumbi ikhadaikhwa Yezu , na mafuta akununkhira akhadasasanyira iwo .
42024002	Iwo agumana mwala wabuluswa pa nthumbi .
42024003	Mbwenye mudapita iwo , hadaagumana manungo a Mbuya Yezu tayu .
42024004	Iwo adzumatirwa napyo , mbacimwana kudziwa pikhafuna iwo kucita . Na mwansanga , aona amuna awiri na nguwo zikhayetimira ninga dzuwa , mbalimira nkhundu mwawo .
42024005	Na kugopa kukhacita iwo , akazi atsolomisa nkhope zawo pantsi , amuna mbaapanga tenepa : “ Thangwi yanji imwe musasaka pakati pa anyakufa , munthu ali m'maso ? ”
42024006	Iye nkhabepo pano ! Alamuka pa kufa ! Kumbukani pikhakupangani Iye mbali na imwe ku dziko ya Galileya kuti :
42024007	“ Ine Mwana wa Munthu ndisafunika kuti ndiperekwe m'manja mwa amuna anyakudawa , ndikhomerwe pa nthanda toera ntsiku ya citatu ndilamuke pa kufa . ”
42024008	Na tenepo , iwo akumbuka mafala a Yezu .
42024009	Mudabwerera iwo buluka ku nthumbi , akazi alonga pinthu pyonsene ipi kuna anyakutumwa khumi na m'bodzi , na kuna onsene anango .
42024010	Akazi adalonga pinthu penepi kuna atumwi a Yezu ndi awa : Mariya Madhalena , Juwana , Mariya mai wace Tiyagu , na akazi anango akhakhala na iwo .
42024011	Mbwenye iwo akhaapokanya akazi . Pikhalonga iwo , akhaabva ninga madzemwa .
42024012	Mbwenye Pedhru alamuka , mbathamanga kwenda ku nthumbi . Mudakotama iye aona nguwo basi . Abuluka mbabwerera na kudzumatirwa na pidacitika .
42024013	Ntsiku ibodzi ene , anyakupfundza awiri a Yezu akhaenda ku cisa cibodzi cinacemerwa Mausi . Kubulukira ku Mausi mpaka ku Djerusalema , pakhali na nsindzo khumi na ubodzi wa makilometuru .
42024014	Mukhaenda iwo na njira , akhaenda mbalonga na thangwi ya pyonsene pikhadacitika .
42024015	Mukhaceza iwo mbakhaketesana , Iye ene Yezu aafendedzera dhuzi mbakhaenda nawo pabodzi .
42024016	Iwo akhamuona , mbwenye akhacimwana kundzindikira .
42024017	Yezu aabvundza tenepa : “ Mphyanji pinafamba imwe mbumuketesana na njira ? ” Iwo alimira na kutsukwala .
42024018	M'bodzi wawo anacemerwa Keleopa , ambvundza kuti : “ Ndiwe wekha basi nfambi mu Djerusalema muno , anacimwana kudziwa pinthu pinacitika mwenemu ntsiku zino ? ”
42024019	Iye abvundzisa kuti : “ Pinthu pyanji ? ” Iwo atawira tenepa : “ Pidacitika na Yezu wa ku Nazareti . Iye akhali mporofeta wa mphambvu pa mafala na pa mabasa , patsogolo pa Mulungu na pa anthu onsene .
42024020	Akulu aanyantsembe pabodzi na atongi athu , ampereka toera aphiwe , mbankhomera pa ntanda .
42024021	Na tenepo , ife tikhadikhira kuti Iye ndiye anadza kafuna kuombola Izaraeli . Pontho na lero kwapita ntsiku zitatu penepyo mbapidamala kucitika kale .
42024022	Akazi anango a pa nsoka wathu , lero atitutumusa . Abesa na macibese ene mbaenda ku nthumbi .
42024023	Kweneko iwo hadaagumana manungo ace tayu . Abwerera mbatipanga kuti ninga ndoto , aona maanju adaapanga kuti Yezu ali m'maso .
42024024	Andzathu anango aenda ku nthumbi , mbagumana pyonsene sawa-sawa ninga mukhadapilongera akazi , mbwenye Yezu hadamuona tayu . ”
42024025	Yezu aapanga tenepa : “ Pisakunentsani tani kubvesesa , pontho mbamudembuka na kutawira pire pyonsene pidalongwa na maporofeta !
42024026	Kodi pikhafunika tayu kuti Kirixtu aone nyatwa zenezi toera apite mu mbiri yace ? ”
42024027	Na tenepo , atoma kuapanga pyonsene pidalembwa m'Bukhu ya Mulungu na thangwi yace , kutomera m'mabukhu a Mozesi na m'mabukhu a maporofeta onsene .
42024028	Pakufika dhuzi na cisa cikhaenda iwo , Yezu acita ninga funa apitirire .
42024029	Mbwenye iwo ankakamiza mbampanga kuti : “ khalani na ife thangwi n'dzidzi wa pita , dzuwa iri kudoka . ” Na tenepo , Iye apita toera akhale na iwo .
42024030	Mukhakhala iwo pa thando ya kudya , Yezu akwata nkate mbapereka takhuta , mbaumenya mbaapasa .
42024031	Na tenepo , maso awo afunguka mbandzindikira , mbwenye Yezu azambazika pa maso pawo .
42024032	Iwo akhalonga okha-okha kuti : “ Kodi mukhaabva tayu mafala ace akhagaka m'mitima mwathu ninga moto mukhalonga Iye n'jira , mbakhatipanga pidalembwa m'bukhu ya Mulungu ? ”
42024033	Iwo alamuka na mwansanga mbabwerera kwenda ku Djerusalema . Kweneko agumana atumwi khumi na m'bodzi na anango akhadagumanyikana ,
42024034	mbakhalonga kuti : “ Ndimo mwene ! Mbuya alamukadi pa kufa , pontho abulukira kuna Simau ! ”
42024035	Na tenepo , ale awiri atoma kulonga pire pidaacitikira njira , pontho mbakhalonga kuti afikira tani kundzindikira pa n'dzidzi ukhamenya Iye nkate .
42024036	Mukhalonga iwo pinthu penepyo , Iye ene Yezu abulukira pakati pawo mbalonga kuti : “ Ntendere mbukhale na imwe ! ”
42024037	Iwo atutumuka , pontho mbagopa mbanyerezera ninga asaona ciphoko .
42024038	Yezu aapanga kuti : Ndi thangwi yanji musadzudzumika , pontho ndi thangwi yanji musapenula m'mitima mwanu ?
42024039	Lang'anani manja anga na myendo yanga . Ndine ene ! Ndiphateni muone . Nzimu nkhabe nyama pontho nkhabe magogodo ninga kuona kunandicita imwe . Ine ndinapyo .
42024040	Pakumala kulonga penepyo , aapangiza manja ace na myendo yace .
42024041	Na kukhonda kutawira kwawo , na thangwi ya ku dzumatirwa na kukomerwa kukhabva iwo , Yezu abvundza kuti : “ Imwe munaco pano cinthu ca kudya ? ”
42024042	Iwo ampasa phindi ibodzi ya nyama ya kuocha ya m'madzi ,
42024043	Iye aikwata mbaidya pa maso pawo .
42024044	Penepo aapanga kuti : “ Ndi penepi pikhakupangani ine mbandiri na imwe . Pikhafunika kuti picitike pyonsene pidalembwa na thangwi yanga mu Mwambo wa Mozesi , m'mabukhu a maporofeta na m'mabukhu a Masalimu . ”
42024045	Na tenepo , aapasa kudzindikira toera akwanise kubvesesa mwadidi pidalembwa m'Bukhu ya Mulungu .
42024046	Mbaapanga tenepa : “ Pyalembwa kuti Kirixtu anati aone nyatwa , mbalamuka pa kufa ingafika ntsiku ya citatu ,
42024047	pontho kuti na dzina Yace , zimwazwe m'madziko onsene , mphangwa za kuchunyuka toera kulekererwa kudawa , kutomera mu Djerusalema .
42024048	Imwe ndimwe amboni a pinthu penepi .
42024049	Ine ndinakutumirani cipikiriro ca Baba wanga . Mbwenye khalani mu nzinda mpaka kudzabza na mphambvu za kudzulu . ”
42024050	Yezu aakwata mbaenda nawo mpaka dhuzi na nzinda wa Bhetanya , kweneko Iye alamusa manja mbaamphemberera .
42024051	Yezu mukhaapasa Iye nkhombo , aasiya , Iye mbakwira kudzulu .
42024052	Na tenepo , iwo amulambira mbabwerera na kutsandzaya kukulu mpaka ku Djerusalema .
42024053	Iwo akhakhala mu Nyumba ya Mulungu midzidzi yonsene mbakhakuza Mulungu .
62001001	Pire pikhalipo kutomera pa kutoma , pire pidabva ife , pire pidaona ife na maso athu , pire pidadingisa ife pontho manja athu mbapiphata , ipi tisapilonga pa thangwi ya Fala ya upulumuki .
62001002	Upulumuki unowu wabulukira . Ife tauona , pontho ndi unowu unacitira ife umboni , mbatikupangani upulumuki wakukhonda kumala ukhali na Baba , pontho mbubulukira kuna ife .
62001003	Ife tisakupangani pire pidaona ife na pidabva ife , toera muphatanembo na ife . Kuphatana kwathu ndi na Mulungu Baba , pontho na Mwana wace Yezu Kirixtu .
62001004	Pontho tisakulemberani pinthu ipi toera kutsandzaya kwathu kudzadziswe .
62001005	Apo mphangwa zidabva ife kuna Kirixtu zinakupangani ife ndi izi : Mulungu ndi cieza . Muna Iye nkhabemo cidima na pang'ono pene .
62001006	Na tenepo , tingalonga kuti taphatana na Mulungu khundu inango mbatifamba n'cidima , dziwani kuti tiri kulonga uthambi mbatikhonda kucita pya ndimo mwene .
62001007	Mbwenye tingafamba mu cieza , ninga Iye ali mu cieza , ife tonsene taphatana m'bodzi na m'bodzi , pontho ciropa ca Yezu Mwana wa Mulungu , cinatitsuka kudawa konsene .
62001008	Tingalonga kuti ife nkhabe kudawa , tiri kunyengezana tekha ene , pontho muna ife nkhabemo pya ndimo mwene .
62001009	Mbwenye tingadambula kudawa kwathu kuna Mulungu , Iye ndi wa kukhulupirika na wakulungama , toera kulekerera kudawa kwathu , na kutitsuka kuipa konsene .
62001010	Tingalonga kuti cipo tidzati kudawa , tisalonga kuti Mulungu ndi nyauthambi , pontho mafala ace nkhabemo muna ife .
62002001	Ananga , ndisakulemberani tsamba iyi toera mukhonde kugwa n'kudawa . Mbwenye munthu m'bodzi angadawa , tinaye munthu wa kutibvunulira patsogolo pana Baba . Ndiye Yezu Kirixtu , Wakulungama .
62002002	Iye ndi ntsembe inafudza madawi athu . Pontho si yakufudza madawi athu basi tayu , mbwenye na madawimbo a anthu onsene .
62002003	Tingabvera matongero ace , tisapangiza kuti tisan'dziwadi Mulungu .
62002004	Ule analonga kuti : “ Ine ndisan'dziwa ” , mbwenye mbakhonda kubvera matongero ace , unowu ndi nyauthambi . Pontho nkhabemo pya ndimo mwene muna iye .
62002005	Mbwenye munthu anabvera mafala ace , kufuna kwa Mulungu kwadzala muna iye . Na tenepo , tisadziwa kuti tiri muna Iye .
62002006	Ule analonga kuti ali kukhala muna Iye , asatongwa kuti afambe ninga Iye .
62002007	Axamwali anga akufunika , matongero awa anakulemberani ine , si mapsa tayu , mbwenye ndi matongero akale ali na imwe kutomera pakutoma . Ndizo Mphangwa zidabva imwe .
62002008	Mbwenye ipi pinakulemberani ine , ndi matongero mapsa . Matongero enewa mba ndimo mwene muna Iye na muna imwe . Thangwi cidima ciri kumala , cieza cakukwana ciri kuyetimira .
62002009	Munthu analonga kuti ali kukhala mu cieza , mbwenye mbaida m'bale wace , unowu adzati kubuluka n'cidima .
62002010	Mphapo ule anafuna m'bale wace , unowu ali mu cieza . Na tenepo , muna iye nkhabe cinthu ca kun'gwegwedusa .
62002011	Mbwenye ule anaida m'bale wace , ali n'cidima , pontho asafamba n'cidima . Na tenepo , nkhabe dziwako kunaenda iye , thangwi cidima campasa udzimola .
62002012	Ananga , ndisakulemberani ipi thangwi kudawa kwanu kwalekererwa , na thangwi ya dzina ya Yezu .
62002013	Ababa na amai , ndisakulemberani ipi thangwi imwe musan'dziwa ule akhalipo kale dziko mbidzati kucitwa . Imwe aphale na atsikana , ndisakulemberani thangwi mwankunda Sathani .
62002014	Ananga , ndakulemberani thangwi musan'dziwa Baba . Ndakulemberani imwe ababa na amai , thangwi imwe musandziwa ule akhalipo kale dziko mbidzati kucitwa . Ndakulemberani imwe aphale na atsikana thangwi imwe ndimwe a mphambvu . Na tenepo mphangwa za Mulungu zina imwe , pontho mwankunda Sathani .
62002015	Lekani kufuna dziko , pontho na pinthu piri n'dziko . Thangwi munthu anafuna dziko , nkhabe kufuna Mulungu Baba .
62002016	Thangwi pyonsene piri pa dziko ninga pinasirira nyama , pinasirira maso , pontho na kupikuza thangwi ya mpfuma , penepi pidabuluka kuna Baba tayu , mbwenye pyabuluka pa dziko .
62002017	Dziko , na pyonsene pire pinasirira iyo pinamala . Mbwenye ule anacita kufuna kwa Mulungu , anakhala kwenda na kwenda .
62002018	Ananga , uno ndi n'dzidzi wakumalisa . Pontho ninga mwapibva kuti nyamalwa wa Kirixtu ali kubwera , apo lero dziwani kuti ali kuoneka azinji anyamalwa a Kirixtu . Na thangwi eneyo , tisadziwa kuti uno ndi n'dzidzi wakumalisa .
62002019	Iwo abuluka muna ife , mbwenye akhali andzathudi tayu . Thangwi mbadakhala andzathu , mbadakhala na ife . Mbwenye na thangwi ya kubuluka kwawo , pisapangiza kuti onsene akhali andzathu tayu .
62002020	Mbwenye imwe mwadzobza na Mulungu , pontho monsene musadziwa .
62002021	Sirikukulemberani na thangwi ya kukhonda dziwa kwanu pinthu pya ndimo mwene tayu , mbwenye thangwi musapidziwa , pontho thangwi musadziwa kuti pinthu pyonsene pya ndimo mwene nkhabe kubala uthambi .
62002022	Mbani nyauthambi ? Ndi ule anakhonda kuti Yezu si Kirixtu tayu . Unowu ndiye nyamalwa wa Kirixtu , ule anakhonda Baba na Mwana ene .
62002023	Onsene anakhonda Mwana , unowu nkhabembo Baba . Mbwenye ule anamulonga pakweca , unowu ana Baba .
62002024	Imwembo koyani m'mitima mwanu pyonsene pidabva imwe kutomera pakutoma . Pire pyonsene pidabva imwe kutomera pa kutoma mungakhala napyo m'mitima mwanu , imwe munati mukhalembo pabodzi na Mwana pontho na Baba .
62002025	Pidatipikirira Iye ndi ipi : Upulumuki wakukhonda kumala .
62002026	Ine ndisakulemberani pinthu ipi , na thangwi ya ale anafuna kukunyengererani .
62002027	Pa thangwi yanu , kudzobza kudatambira imwe kuna iye kuli muna imwe , pontho nkhabe funika munthu akupfundziseni . Mbwenye ninga kudzobza kwace kudatambira imwe muna Iye nkhwa ndimo mwene si kwa uthambi tayu , kunakupfundzisani pa thangwi ya pinthu pyonsene . Khalani muna Iye ninga mudakupfundzisirani Iye .
62002028	Ananga , cincino khalani muna Kirixtu , toera Iye angapangizika tin'nyindire , tikhonde kupasika manyadzo pa maso pace , pa kubwera kwace .
62002029	Ngakhala imwe musadziwa kuti Yezu ndi wakulungama , dziwanimbo kuti onsene ale anacita pyakulungama abalwa na Mulungu .
62003001	Lang'anani kutifuna kukulu kudacita Baba , na kuticita kuti ife ticemerwe ana a Mulungu . Ndimo mwene ndifedi ana a Mulungu . Ndi thangwi eneyo dziko nkhabe kutidziwa , thangwi iyo nkhabe kun'dziwambo tayu .
62003002	Axamwali akufunika , ife cincino ndife ana a Mulungu , pontho pidzati kudziwika kuti tinadza kakhala tani . Mbwenye tisadziwa kuti Kirixtu angadza kapangizika , ife tinadza kalandana naye . Thangwi tinadza kamuona kukhala kudacita iye .
62003003	Mphapo munthu onsene ana cidikhiro ceneci muna Kirixtu , asatongwa kuti akhale wakulungama , sawa-sawa ninga Kirixtu ndi wakulungama .
62003004	Munthu onsene anacita kudawa , anumpha Mwambo wa Mulungu . Ndimo mwene , kudawa nkhunumpha Mwambo .
62003005	Imwe musapidziwa kuti Kirixtu abwera kudza kabulusa madawi athu , pontho muna Iye nkhabe kudawa .
62003006	Onsene ale anakhala muna Kirixtu , nkhabe kukhala n'kudawa . Onsene ale anakhala n'kudawa , adzati kumuona , pontho adzati kun'dziwa .
62003007	Ananga , lekani kunyengezwa na munthu . Ule anacita pinthu pyakulungama ndi wakulungama , sawa-sawa ninga Kirixtu ndi wakulungama .
62003008	Apo ule anakhala mbadawa , unowu ndi munthu wa Sathani . Thangwi Sathani adza mbadawa kutomera kale na kale . Ndi thangwi eneyo Mwana wa Mulungu abwera , toera kufudza mabasa a Sathani .
62003009	Onsene adabalwa na Mulungu nkhabe kukhala mbacita kudawa , thangwi mbeu ya Mulungu iri muna iye . Na tenepo , unowu nkhabe kwanisa kukhala mbacita kudawa , thangwi abalwa na Mulungu .
62003010	Na mwenemu , tisadziwa mbani ana a Mulungu , peno mbani ana a Sathani . Onsene ale anakhonda kucita pinthu pyakulungama , na onsene anakhonda kufuna m'bale wace , hadabuluka kuna Mulungu tayu .
62003011	Izi ndizo mphangwa zidabva imwe kutomera pa kutoma kuti : Tifunane m'bodzi na m'bodzi .
62003012	Mbatilekeni kukhala ninga Kainu , munthu wa Sathani adapha m'bale wace . Apo thangwi yanji iye apha m'bale wace ? Amupha thangwi mabasa ace akhali akuipa , mbwenye mabasa a m'bale wace akhali akulungama .
62003013	Abale anga , lekani kudzudzumika mungazondiwa na dziko .
62003014	Tisadziwa kuti ife tabuluka pa kufa , mbwenye cincino tapulumuka thangwi tisafuna abale athu . Mphapo ule anakhonda funa m'bale wace , ali n'kufa .
62003015	Munthu onsene anazonda m'bale wace ndi phanga . Pontho imwe musadziwa kuti phanga nkhabe upulumuki wakukhonda kumala muna iye .
62003016	Na mwenemu , ife tisadziwa ndi ninji kufunana , thangwi Yezu Kirixtu apereka upulumuki wace na thangwi yathu . Na tenepo , ife tisatongwambo kupereka upulumuki wathu na thangwi ya abale athu .
62003017	Munthu wa kupfuma mbaona m'bale wace ali kucherenga mbakhonda kumphedza , munthu unowu analonga kuti asafuna Mulungu ?
62003018	Ananga , kufunana kwathu mbukuleke kukhala kwa mafala na mulomo basi tayu , mbwenye mbukukhale kwa mabasa na mwa ndimo mwene .
62003019	Na tenepo , tinadziwa kuti ife ndife a ndimo mwene , pontho tinakhurudzisa ntima wathu patsogolo pana Mulungu ,
62003020	ntima wathu ungatipanga kuti tadawa . Mulungu ndi nkulu kakamwe kupita ntima wathu , pontho asadziwa pinthu pyonsene .
62003021	Axamwali anga akufunika , ntima wathu ungakhonda kutipanga kuti tadawa , tina cinyindiro patsogolo pana Mulungu .
62003022	Pontho pyonsene pinaphemba ife anatipasa , thangwi tisabvera matongero ace pontho tisacita pinafuna Iye .
62003023	Matongero ace ndi awa : Kuti titawire dzina ya Yezu Kirixtu Mwana wace , pontho tifunane m'bodzi na m'bodzi , ninga mudatipangira Iye .
62003024	Ale anabvera matongero a Mulungu , asakhala muna Mulungu , Mulungumbo asakhala muna iwo . Na tenepo , tisadziwa kuti Iye asakhala muna ife , na thangwi ya Nzimu udatipasa Iye .
62004001	Axamwali akufunika , lekani kubvera mizimu yonsene , mbwenye ilang'aniseni mwadidi toera muione ngakhala yabuluka kuna Mulungu . Thangwi aporofeta azinji a uthambi ali kubalalika n'dziko muno .
62004002	Nzimu wa Mulungu imwe munakwanisa kuudzindikira tenepa : Nzimu onsene unalonga kuti Yezu Kirixtu acitika munthu , nzimu unowu wabuluka kuna Mulungu .
62004003	Mbwenye nzimu onsene unakhonda kulonga penepi , hudabuluka kuna Mulungu tayu . Unowu ndi nzimu wa nyamalwa wa Kirixtu , ule udabva imwe kale kuti uli kubwera , apo cincino uli pano pa dziko .
62004004	Ananga , imwe ndimwe a Mulungu , pontho mwaikunda mizimu ya uthambi . Thangwi ule ali muna imwe ana mphambvu kupita ule ali pa dziko .
62004005	Iwo abuluka n'dziko . Na thangwi eneyo , pire pinalonga iwo pisabuluka n'dziko , pontho dziko isaabvera .
62004006	Ife tabuluka kuna Mulungu , pontho onsene ale anadziwa Mulungu asatibvera . Mbwenye ule anakhonda buluka kuna Mulungu , nkhabe kutibvera . Na tenepo tisakwanisa kudzindikira Nzimu wa ndimo mwene , na nzimu wa uthambi .
62004007	Axamwali akufunika , mbatifunaneni m'bodzi na m'bodzi , thangwi kufunana kusabuluka kuna Mulungu . Ule anafuna ndzace , abalwa na Mulungu , pontho asan'dziwa Mulungu .
62004008	Mphapo ule anakhonda kufuna ndzace nkhabe kun'dziwa Mulungu , thangwi Mulungu ndi kufunana .
62004009	Mulungu apangiza kufuna kwace pakati pathu tenepa : Atuma Mwana wace m'bodzi ekha pa dziko , toera iye aticite kuti tikhale m'maso .
62004010	Kufunana kwacitika tenepa : Sife adafuna Mulungu tayu , mbwenye ndiye adatifuna mbatitumira Mwana wace , toera kufudza madawi athu .
62004011	Axamwali anga akufunika , na kutifuna kudaticita Mulungu , ifembo tisatongwa tifunane m'bodzi na m'bodzi .
62004012	Cipo nkhabe munthu adaona Mulungu . Mphapo tingafunana m'bodzi na m'bodzi , Mulungu anakhala muna ife , pontho kufuna kwace kunadzaleratu kakamwe muna ife .
62004013	Ife tisadziwa kuti tiri muna Mulungu , Iyembo ali muna ife , thangwi Iye atipasa Nzimu wace .
62004014	Na tenepo , ife tamuona , pontho tisaenda mbatilonga umboni kuti Baba atuma Mwana wace , toera akhale Mpulumusi wa dziko .
62004015	Munthu analonga pakweca kuti Yezu ndi Mwana wa Mulungu , munthu unowu Mulungu anakhala muna iye , iyembo anakhala muna Mulungu .
62004016	Na tenepo , ife tisadziwa kutifuna kunaticita Mulungu , pontho kutifuna kweneku tisanyindirako . Mulungu ndi kufunana . Onsene anakhala mwa kufunana ali muna Mulungu , pontho Mulungu ali muna iye .
62004017	Na tenepo , kufunana kwadzala pakati pathu toera ntsiku ya kutongwa tikhale na kunyindira . Thangwi pa dziko ino ndife sawa-sawa ninga Yezu .
62004018	Pana kufunana nkhabe gumanika kugopa . Pontho kufunana kwakukwana kusamalisa kugopa . Thangwi ale anagopa , asagopa nyatwa . Ule anagopa nkhabe kufunana kwakukwana .
62004019	Ife tisanfuna , thangwi Iye ndiye adatifuna pakutoma .
62004020	Munthu analonga kuti : “ Ine ndisafuna Mulungu ” , mbwenye mbaida m'bale wace , unowu ndi nyauthambi . Thangwi munthu anakhonda funa m'bale wace anaona iye na maso ace , anacimwana kufuna Mulungu anakhonda kuona iye .
62004021	Mulungu atisiyira matongero awa : Kuti ule anafuna Mulungu , mbafunembo m'bale wace .
62005001	Munthu onsene anatawira kuti Yezu ndi Kirixtu , unowu abalwa na Mulungu . Pontho munthu onsene anafuna Baba , mbafunembo Mwana wace .
62005002	Tingafuna Mulungu mbatibvera matongero ace , penepi ndipyo pinapangiza kuti tisaafuna ana a Mulungu .
62005003	Thangwi kufuna Mulungu nkhubvera matongero ace , pontho matongero ace nkhabe lemera .
62005004	Thangwi ule anabalwa na Mulungu asakunda dziko . Tisakwanisa kukunda dziko na kukhulupira kwathu .
62005005	Ndi ani anakwanisa kukunda dziko ? Ndi ule basi anatawira kuti Yezu ndi Mwana wa Mulungu .
62005006	Yezu Kirixtu ndi unowu adabwera na madzi na ciropa . Si na madzi basi tayu , mbwenye ndi na madzi na ciropa . Pontho Nzimu wa Mulungu ndiwo unacita umboni , thangwi Nzimu wa Mulungu ndi wa ndimo mwene .
62005007	Piripo pinthu pitatu pinacita umboni [ kudzulu . Baba , Fala na Nzimu wa Mulungu . Pitatu ipi , pisabverana .
62005008	Pontho pitatu ipi ndipyo pinacita umboni pa dziko . ] Nzimu wa Mulungu , madzi na ciropa . Pitatu ipi , ndi cinthu cibodzi basi .
62005009	Ife tisatawira umboni wa anthu , mbwenye umboni wa Mulungu ndiwo ukulu , thangwi ndi umboni unacitira iye Mwana wace .
62005010	Munthu anatawira Mwana wa Mulungu anawo umboni unowu mu ntima mwace . Mbwenye ule anakhonda kutawira Mulungu , asacita Mulungu ninga ndi nyauthambi . Thangwi asakhonda umboni udatipasa Mulungu na thangwi ya Mwana wace .
62005011	Umboni wa Mulungu ndi uyu : Kuti Mulungu atipasa upulumuki wakukhonda kumala . Upulumuki unowu uli muna Mwana wace .
62005012	Ule ana Mwana wa Mulungu , anawo upulumuki . Mbwenye anasowa Mwana wa Mulungu , nkhabe upulumuki .
62005013	Ine ndakulemberani pyonsene ipi , toera imwe mudatawira dzina ya Mwana wa Mulungu , mudziwe kuti munawo upulumuki wakukhonda kumala .
62005014	Cinyindiro cina ife muna Iye ndi ici : Kuti tingamphemba cinthu ninga munafunira Iye , Iye asatibva .
62005015	Pontho tingadziwa kuti Iye asatibva pa pyonsene pinamphemba ife , tisadziwa kuti tapasiwa pyonsene pidamphemba ife .
62005016	Munthu anaona m'bale wace mbacita kudawa kunakhonda kubala kufa , mbamphemberere , Mulungu anampulumusa . Penepi ndisalongera kuna ale kuti kudawa kwawo nkhabe kubala kufa . Thangwi kulipo kudawa kunabala kufa . Sirikulonga enewa tayu . Kuna anthu enewa , lekani kuaphemberera .
62005017	Pinthu pyonsene pyakukhonda kulungama ndi kudawa . Mbwenye kulipo kudawa kunakhonda kubala kufa .
62005018	Tisadziwa kuti onsene adabalwa na Mulungu nkhabe kukhala n'kudawa , thangwi Mwana wa Mulungu anaakoya . Na tenepo , Sathani nkhabe kuacita kuipa .
62005019	Tisadziwa kuti ife ndife a Mulungu , pontho dziko yonsene isatongwa na Sathani .
62005020	Tisadziwambo kuti Mwana wa Mulungu abwera mbatipasa ndzeru toera tidziwe Mulungu wa ndimo mwene . Pontho ife tiri muna Mulungu wa ndimo mwene , muna Mwana wace Yezu Kirixtu . Yezu Kirixtu unowu , ndiye Mulungudi na upulumuki wakukhonda kumala .
62005021	Ananga , citani mphole na alungu apezi .
63001001	Ine ntsogoleri ,  ndisalemba tsamba iyi kuna mai adasankhulwa , na kuna anace anafunikadi na ine kakamwe . Sine basi tayu anaafuna , mbwenye asafuniwambo na onsene ale anadziwa pya ndimo mwene ,
63001002	na thangwi ya pya ndimo mwene pinakhala muna ife , pontho piri na ife kwenda na kwenda .
63001003	Ntsisi , kukoma ntima , na ntendere wa Mulungu Baba na wa Mwana wace Yezu Kirixtu , mbapikhale na ife mwa ndimo mwene na mwakufunana .
63001004	Ndakomerwa pikulu kakamwe pidagumana ine anako anango mbafamba mwakulungama , ninga munalongera mwambo udatambira ife kuna Baba .
63001005	Cincino ndisakuphembani mai , kuti tifunane m'bodzi na m'bodzi . Si kuti ndiri kukulemberani mwambo upsa tayu . Mbwenye mwambo unowu ndiwo ukhali na ife kutomera pa kutoma .
63001006	Kufunana ndi uku : Kuti tifambe ninga munalongera matongero ace . Ninga mwaabva kale na kale , matongero ace ndi awa : Kuti mufambe na kufunana kweneku .
63001007	Ndimo mwene , alipo anyauthambi azinji asabulukira pa dziko , mbakhonda kuti Yezu Kirixtu acitika munthu . Anthu enewa ndiwo anyauthambi na anyamalwa a Kirixtu .
63001008	Citani mphole , gopa munadza kaluza misapu ya basa yathu , mbwenye toera mupaswe m'bairo wanu wamumphu .
63001009	Onsene ale anakhonda kukhala mu cipfundzo ca Kirixtu mbwenye mbabuluka kunja , enewa nkhabe Mulungu . Ule anakhala mu cipfundzo ca Kirixtu , ana Baba pontho ana Mwana .
63001010	Munthu anadza kuna imwe mbakhonda kudza na cipfundzo ceneci , lekani kuntambira pa nyumba panu , pontho lekani kum'mwanyika .
63001011	Thangwi ule anam'mwanyika anaphatana na iye pa mabasa ace a kuipa .
63001012	Ndina pizinji kuti ndikulembereni , mbwenye sikhafuna kuti ndicite kupilemba pa tsamba tayu . Thangwi ndisadikhira kudza kakuonani toera ndilonge na imwe nkhope na nkhope , toera kutsandzaya kwathu kudzadziswe .
63001013	Ana a mwana-nkazi wako wakusankhulwa , asakuwangisa .
64001001	Ine ntsogoleri ,  ndisalemba tsamba iyi kuna wakufunika Gayo , unowu anafuna ine kakamwe .
64001002	Xamwali wanga wakufunika , ndisaphembera kuti ukhale manungo akuwanga , pyonsene pikufambire mwadidi , ninga nzimu wako uli mwadidi .
64001003	Ndatsandzaya pikulu kakamwe mudatambira ine abale anango mbandipanga na thangwi ya kukhulupira kwako , na kufamba mwa ndimo mwene kunacita iwe .
64001004	Nkhabe kutsandzaya kunango kwa ine , kunapiringana kubva kudacita ine kuti ananga ali kufamba mwakulungama .
64001005	Xamwali wanga wakufunika , iwe ndiwe wakukhulupirika pa pire pinacita iwe kuli abale , iwo mbakhala anthu anakhonda iwe kudziwa .
64001006	Iwo acita umboni pa maso pa abale anyakutawira Yezu , mbalonga na thangwi ya kukoma ntima kwako . Mphyadidi uwaphedze kufamba pa ulendo wawo , toera Mulungu atsandzaye napyo .
64001007	Thangwi na dzina ya Yezu , iwo abuluka , mbakhonda tawira kuphebza cinthu cibodzi na ale adakhonda kutawira Yezu .
64001008	Thangwi tisatongwa tiatambire na ntsisi abale ninga enewa , toera tikhale anthu akuphatana pa kuphata basa ya kumwaza pya ndimo mwene .
64001009	Ndalemba tsamba kuna abale anyakutawira Yezu , mbwenye Dhiyoterefi , na kufuna kwace ukulu pa nsoka wawo , akhonda kutitambira .
64001010	Na tenepo , ine ndingafika kweneku ndinansandika , na thangwi ya pinacita iye na mafala ace a kuipa anatilongera iye . Mbwenye iye nkhabe komerwa basi na penepi tayu . Abale angafika kweneku iye nkhabe kuatambira . Pontho munthu unango angafuna kuatambira , iye asan'khondesa mpaka kufikira kun'thamangisa pa nsoka wa abale anyakutawira Yezu .
64001011	Xamwali wanga wakufunika , leka towerera pya kuipa , mbwenye towerera pyadidi . Ule anacita pyadidi ndi wa Mulungu , mbwenye ule anacita pya kuipa adzati kuona Mulungu .
64001012	Mbwenye Dhemetiryo , anthu onsene asansimba . Pyamaso pinaphata iye pisancitira umboni . Na ifeenembo tisancitira umboni . Pontho iwe usadziwa kuti umboni wathu ndi wa ndimo mwene .
64001013	Ndikhali na pinthu pizinji pya kufuna kukulembera , mbwenye sinafuna cita kupilemba tayu ,
64001014	thangwi ndisafuna kudza kakuona cincino . Na tenepo , tinadza kaceza mwadidi tingadza kaonana nkhope na nkhope .
64001015	Ntendere mbukhale na iwe . Axamwali a kuno asakuwangisa . Wangisambo axamwali a kweneko , m'bodzi na m'bodzi .
